# Veremos los primeros 12 nombres de regiones en country.map

install.packages("choroplethrMaps")
install.packages("gapminder")

install.packages("Rcpp")

library(gapminder)
library(dplyr)
library(ggmap)
library(ggplot2)
library(Rcpp)

data(country.map, package = "choroplethrMaps")
head(unique(country.map$region), 12)

# preparar conjunto de datos

data(gapminder, package = "gapminder")
plotdata <- gapminder %>%
  filter(year == 2007) %>%
  rename(region = country,
         value = lifeExp) %>%
  mutate(region = tolower(region)) %>%
  mutate(region = recode(region,
                         "united states"    = "Estados Unidos",
                         "congo, dem. rep." = "Replubica democrata del Congo",
                         "congo, rep."      = "Republica de Congo",
                         "korea, dem. rep." = "Sur Korea",
                         "korea. rep."      = "Nort korea",
                         "tanzania"         = "Republica unida de Tanzania",
                         "serbia"           = "Republica de Serbia",
                         "slovak republic"  = "Slovakia",
                         "yemen, rep."      = "Yemen"))
